Post-Quantum Cryptographic Algorithms\n\n### 2.1 NIST-Standardized PQC Algorithms\n\n#### Crystals-Kyber (Key Encapsulation Mechanism)\n```python\n# Crystals-Kyber Implementation\nclass CrystalsKyberKEM:\n    """\n    NIST-standardized lattice-based KEM\n    Security Level: 128-bit (Kyber512), 192-bit (Kyber768), 256-bit (Kyber1024)\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, self._sample_polynomial(self.eta2)\n        \n        # Compute public key: t = A * s + e\n        t = self._matrix_vector_multiply(A, s)\n        t = self._add_polynomials(t, e)\n        \n        # Serialize keys\n        pk = self._serialize_public_key(A, t)\n        sk = self._serialize_private_key(s)\n        \n        return pk, sk\n    \n    def encapsulate(self, pk: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Encapsulate shared secret"""\n        # Deserialize public key\n        A, t = self._deserialize_public_key(pk)\n        \n        # Generate random message and error\n        m = self._sample_message()\n        e1 = self._sample_polynomial(self.eta2)\n        e2 = self._sample_polynomial(self.eta2)\n        \n        # Compute ciphertext\n        u = self._matrix_vector_multiply(A, m)\n        u = self._add_polynomials(u, e1)\n        \n        v = self._inner_product(t, m)\n        v = self._add_polynomials(v, e2)\n        \n        # Derive shared secret\n        ss = self._kdf(m, u, v)\n        \n        # Serialize ciphertext\n        ct = self._serialize_ciphertext(u, v)\n        \n        return ct, ss\n    \n    def decapsulate(self, ct: bytes, sk: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Decapsulate shared secret"""\n        # Deserialize private key and ciphertext\n        s = self._deserialize_private_key(sk)\n        u, v = self._deserialize_ciphertext(ct)\n        \n        # Recover message\n        m_prime = self._recover_message(s, u, v)\n        \n        # Derive shared secret\n        ss = self._kdf(m_prime, CrystalsDilithiumSignature:\n    """\n    NIST-standardized lattice-based signature scheme\n    Security Level: 128-bit (Dilithium2), 192-bit (Dilithium3), 256-bit (Dilithium5)\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, security_level: int = 256):\n        self.security_level = security_level\n        self.n = 256  # Polynomial degree\n        self.k = self._get_k(security_level)\n        self.l = self._get_l(security_level)\n        self.eta = self._get_eta(security_level)\n        self.gamma1 = self._get_gamma1(security_level)\n        self.gamma2 = self._get_gamma2(security_level)\n        self.tau = self._get_tau(security_level)\n        self.beta = self._get_beta(security_level)\n        \n    def keygen(self) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Generate public/private key pair"""\n        # Generate matrix A\n        A = self._generate_matrix()\n        \n        # Generate secret vectors s1, s2\n        s1 = [self._sample_polynomial(self.eta) for _ in range(self.l)]\n        s2 = [self._sample_polynomial(self.eta) for _ in range(self.k)]\n        \n        # Compute t = A * s1 + s2\n        t = self._compute_t(A, s1, s2)\n        \n        # Compute public key\n        rho = self._generate_seed()\n        tr = self._hash(rho)\n        t0 = self._power2round(t)\n        pk = self._serialize_public_key(rho, t0, tr)\n        \n        # Compute private key\n        sk = self._serialize_private_key(rho, tr, s1, s2, t0)\n        \n        return pk, sk\n    \n    def sign(self, message: bytes, sk: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Generate signature for message"""\n        # Deserialize private key\n        rho, tr, s1, s2, t0 = self._deserialize_private_key(sk)\n        \n        # Compute matrix A from seed rho\n        A = self._expand_matrix(rho)\n        \n        # Compute mu = H(tr || message)\n        mu = self._hash(tr + message)\n        \n        # Rejection sampling loop\n        while True:\n            # Generate random kappa\n            kappa = self._generate_random()\n            \n            # Compute y = H(kappa || mu)\n            y = self._expand_y(kappa, mu)\n            \n            # Compute w = A * y\n            w = self._compute_w(A, y)\n            \n            # Compute w1 = HighBits(w)\n            w1 = self._high_bits(w, 2 * self.gamma1)\n            \n            # Compute c = H(mu || w1)\n            c = self._hash(mu + self._serialize(w1))\n            \n            # Compute z = y + c * s1\n            z = self._compute_z(y, c, s1)\n            \n            # Compute c0 = LowBits(c * t, 2 * self.gamma2)\n            ct = self._compute_ct(c, t0)\n            c0 = self._low_bits(ct, 2 * self.gamma2)\n            \n            # Check rejection conditions\n            if self._check_rejection(z, ct):\n                # Compute h = H(kappa)\n                h = self._hash(kappa)\n                \n                # Serialize signature\n                sig = self._serialize_signature(c, z, h, c0)\n                \n                return sig\n    \n    def verify(self, message: bytes, signature: bytes, pk: bytes) -> bool:\n        """Verify signature"""\n        # Deserialize public key and signature\n        rho, t0, tr = self._deserialize_public_key(pk)\n        c, z, h, c0 = self._deserialize_signature(signature)\n        \n        # Compute matrix A from seed rho\n        A = self._expand_matrix(rho)\n        \n        # Compute mu = H(tr || message)\n        mu = self._hash(tr + message)\n        \n        # Compute w1\' = HighBits(A * z - c * t0, 2 * self.gamma1)\n        Az = self._compute_w(A, [z])\n        ct0 = self._compute_ct_vector(c, t0)\n        w1_prime = self._high_bits(self._subtract(Az, ct0), 2 * self.gamma1)\n        \n        # Compute c\' = H(mu || w1\')\n        c_prime = self._hash(mu + self._serialize(w1_prime))\n        \n        # Verify c == c\'\n        if c != c_prime:\n            return False\n        \n        # Verify z norm\n        if not self._verify_z_norm(z):\n            return False\n        \n        # Verify c0 norm\n        if not self._verify_c0_norm(c0):\n            return False\n        \n        return True\n    \n    def _get_k(self, security_level: int) -> int:\n        """Get k parameter based on security level"""\n        if security_level == 128:\n            return 4\n        elif security_level == 192:\n            return 6\n        else:  # 256\n            return 8\n    \n    def _get_l(self, security_level: int) -> int:\n        """Get l parameter based on security Signature)\n```python\n# SPHINCS+ Implementation\nclass SphincsPlusSignature:\n    """\n    NIST-standardized stateless hash-based signature scheme\n    Security Level: 128-bit (SPHINCS+-128s), 192-bit (SPHINCS+-192s), 256-bit (SPHINCS+-256s)\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, security_level: int = 256, variant: str = "simple"):\n        self.security_level = security_level\n        self.variant = variant  # "simple" or "robust"\n        self.n = self._get_n(security_level)\n        self.m = self._get_m(security_level)\n        self.h = self._get_h(security_level)\n        self.d = self._get_d(security_level)\n        self.w = self._get_w(security_level)\n        \n    def keygen(self) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Generate public/private key pair"""\n        # Generate seed\n        sk_seed = self._generate_seed()\n        pk_seed = self._generate_seed()\n        \n        # Compute public key\n        pk = self._compute_public_key(sk_seed, pk_seed)\n        \n        # Serialize keys\n        sk = self._serialize_private_key(sk_seed, pk_seed)\n        pk_bytes = self._serialize_public_key(pk_seed, pk)\n        \n        return pk_bytes, sk\n    \n    def sign(self, message: bytes, sk: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Generate signature for message"""\n        # Deserialize private key\n        sk_seed, pk_seed = self._deserialize_private_key(sk)\n        \n        # Compute message digest\n        M = self._hash(message)\n        \n        # Compute randomizer\n        r = self._prf(sk_seed, M)\n        \n        # Compute tree index and leaf index\n        tree_idx, leaf_idx = self._compute_indices(r)\n        \n        # Compute WOTS+ signature\n        sig_wots = self._wots_sign(M, sk_seed, pk_seed, tree_idx, leaf_idx)\n        \n        # Compute authentication path\n        auth_path = self._compute_auth_path(sk_seed, pk_seed, tree_idx, leaf_idx)\n        \n        # Serialize signature\n        sig = self._serialize_signature(r, sig_wots, auth_path)\n        \n        return sig\n    \n    def verify(self, message: bytes, signature: bytes, pk: bytes) -> bool:\n        """Verify signature"""\n        # Deserialize public key and signature\n        pk_seed, pk_root = self._deserialize_public_key(pk)\n        r, sig_wots, auth_path = self._deserialize_signature(signature)\n        \n        # Compute message digest\n        M = self._hash(message)\n        \n        # Compute tree index and leaf index\n        tree_idx, leaf_idx = self._compute_indices(r)\n        \n        # Compute WOTS+ public key\n        pk_wots = self._wots_pk_from_sig(M, r, sig_wots, pk_seed)\n        \n        # Compute leaf hash\n        leaf = self._hash_leaf(pk_wots, leaf_idx)\n        \n        # Compute root from authentication path\n        root_computed = self._compute_root(leaf, auth_path, tree_idx, leaf_idx, pk_seed)\n        \n        # Verify root matches public key\n        return root_computed == pk_root\n    \n    def _get_n(self, security_level: int) -> int:\n        """Get n parameter based on security level"""\n        if security_level == 128:\n            return 16\n        elif security_level == 192:\n            return 24\n        else:  # 256\n            return 32\n    \n    def _get_m(self, security_level: int) -> int:\n        """Get m parameter based on security level"""\n        if security_level == 128:\n            return 16\n        elif security_level == 192:\n            return 24\n        else:  # 256\n            return 32\n    \n    def _get_h(self, security_level: int) -> int:\n        """Get h parameter based on security level"""\n        if security_level == 128:\n            return 63\n        elif security_level == 192:\n            return 66\n        else:  # 256\n            return 67\n    \n    def _get_d(self, security_level: int) -> int:\n        """Get d parameter based on security level"""\n        if security_level == 128:\n            return 7\n        elif security_level == 192:\n            return 22\n        else:  # 256\n            return 22\n    \n    def _get_w(self, security_level: int) -> int:\n        """Get w parameter based on security level"""\n        if security_level == 128:\n            return 16\n        elif security_level == 192:\n            return 16\n        else:  # 256\n            return 16\n    \n    def _generate_seed(self) -> bytes:\n        """Generate random seed"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _compute_public_key(self, sk_seed: bytes, pk_seed: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Compute public key from seeds"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _serialize_private_key(self, sk_seed: bytes, pk_seed: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Serialize private key"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _deserialize_private_key(self, sk: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Deserialize private key"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _serialize_public_key(self, pk_seed: bytes, pk: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Serialize public key"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _deserialize_public_key(self, pk: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Deserialize public key"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _hash(self, data: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Hash function using SHAKE256"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _prf(self, key: bytes, data: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Pseudo-random function"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _compute_indices(self, r: bytes) -> Tuple[int, int]:\n        """Compute tree and leaf indices"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _wots_sign(self, M: bytes, sk_seed: bytes, pk_seed: bytes, \n                   tree_idx: int, leaf_idx: int) -> bytes:\n        """Compute WOTS+ signature"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _compute_auth_path(self, sk_seed: bytes, pk_seed: bytes, \n                           tree_idx: int, leaf_idx: int) -> bytes:\n        """Compute authentication path"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _serialize_signature(self, r: bytes, sig_wots: bytes, \n                             auth_path: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Serialize signature"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _deserialize_signature(self, sig: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes, bytes]:\n        """Deserialize signature"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _wots_pk_from_sig(self, M: bytes, r: bytes, sig_wots: bytes, \n                          pk_seed: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Compute WOTS+ public key from signature"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _hash_leaf(self, pk_wots: bytes, leaf_idx: int) -> bytes:\n        """Hash leaf node"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _compute_root(self, leaf: bytes, auth_path: bytes, tree_idx: int, \n                      leaf_idx: int, pk_seed: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Compute root from authentication path"""\n        pass\n\n\n# Performance Encryption\n```python\n# Hybrid Cryptographic Architecture\nclass HybridCryptographicSystem:\n    """\n    Hybrid cryptographic system combining classical and post-quantum algorithms\n    Provides security against both classical and quantum attacks\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, classical_algorithm: str = "RSA-4096", \n                 pq_algorithm: str = "Kyber1024"):\n        self.classical_algorithm = classical_algorithm\n        self.pq_algorithm = pq_algorithm\n        \n        # Initialize classical crypto\n        if classical_algorithm == "RSA-4096":\n            self.classical_crypto = RSA4096()\n        elif classical_algorithm == "ECC-P521":\n            self.classical_crypto = ECCP521()\n        \n        # Initialize post-quantum crypto\n        if pq_algorithm == "Kyber1024":\n            self.pq_crypto = CrystalsKyberKEM(security_level=256)\n        elif pq_algorithm == "NTRU":\n            self.pq_crypto = NTRUEncrypt()\n    \n    def hybrid_keygen(self) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Generate hybrid public/private key pair"""\n        # Generate classical keys\n        classical_pk, classical_sk = self.classical_crypto.keygen()\n        \n        # Generate post-quantum keys\n        pq_pk, pq_sk = self.pq_crypto.keygen()\n        \n        # Combine keys\n        hybrid_pk = self._combine_public_keys(classical_pk, pq_pk)\n        hybrid_sk = self._combine_private_keys(classical_sk, pq_sk)\n        \n        return hybrid_pk, hybrid_sk\n    \n    def hybrid_encapsulate(self, hybrid_pk: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Encapsulate shared secret using hybrid scheme"""\n        # Split public key\n        classical_pk, pq_pk = self._split_public_key(hybrid_pk)\n        \n        # Encapsulate with classical algorithm\n        classical_ct, classical_ss = self.classical_crypto.encapsulate(classical_pk)\n        \n        # Encapsulate with post-quantum algorithm\n        pq_ct, pq_ss = self.pq_crypto.encapsulate(pq_pk)\n        \n        # Combine ciphertexts\n        hybrid_ct = self._combine_ciphertexts(classical_ct, pq_ct)\n        \n        # Derive final shared secret\n        final_ss = self._derive_shared_secret(classical_ss, pq_ss)\n        \n        return hybrid_ct, final_ss\n    \n    def hybrid_decapsulate(self, hybrid_ct: bytes, hybrid_sk: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Decapsulate shared secret using hybrid scheme"""\n        # Split private key and ciphertext\n        classical_sk, pq_sk = self._split_private_key(hybrid_sk)\n        classical_ct, pq_ct = self._split_ciphertext(hybrid_ct)\n        \n        # Decapsulate with classical algorithm\n        classical_ss = self.classical_crypto.decapsulate(classical_ct, classical_sk)\n        \n        # Decapsulate with post-quantum algorithm\n        pq_ss = self.pq_crypto.decapsulate(pq_ct, pq_sk)\n        \n        # Derive final shared secret\n        final_ss = self._derive_shared_secret(classical_ss, pq_ss)\n        \n        return final_ss\n    \n    def _combine_public_keys(self, classical_pk: bytes, pq_pk: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Combine classical and post-quantum public keys"""\n        # Format: [length][classical_pk][pq_pk]\n        length = len(classical_pk) + len(pq_pk)\n        return length.to_bytes(4, \'big\') + classical_pk + pq_pk\n    \n    def _split_public_key(self, hybrid_pk: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Split hybrid public key"""\n        length = int.from_bytes(hybrid_pk[:4], \'big\')\n        classical_pk = hybrid_pk[4:4+len(classical_pk)]\n        pq_pk = hybrid_pk[4+len(classical_pk):]\n        return classical_pk, pq_pk\n    \n    def _combine_private_keys(self, classical_sk: bytes, pq_sk: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Combine classical and post-quantum private keys"""\n        # Format: [length][classical_sk][pq_sk]\n        length = len(classical_sk) + len(pq_sk)\n        return length.to_bytes(4, \'big\') + classical_sk + pq_sk\n    \n    def _split_private_key(self, hybrid_sk: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Split hybrid private key"""\n        length = int.from_bytes(hybrid_sk[:4], \'big\')\n        classical_sk = hybrid_sk[4:4+len(classical_sk)]\n        pq_sk = hybrid_sk[4+len(classical_sk):]\n        return classical_sk, pq_sk\n    \n    def _combine_ciphertexts(self, classical_ct: bytes, pq_ct: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Combine classical and post-quantum ciphertexts"""\n        # Format: [length][classical_ct][pq_ct]\n        length = len(classical_ct) + len(pq_ct)\n        return length.to_bytes(4, \'big\') + classical_ct + pq_ct\n    \n    def _split_ciphertext(self, hybrid_ct: bytes) -> Tuple[bytes, bytes]:\n        """Split hybrid ciphertext"""\n        length = int.from_bytes(hybrid_ct[:4], \'big\')\n        classical_ct = hybrid_ct[4:4+len(classical_ct)]\n        pq_ct = hybrid_ct[4+len(classical_ct):]\n        return classical_ct, pq_ct\n    \n    def _derive_shared_secret(self, classical_ss: bytes, pq_ss: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Derive final shared secret from both secrets"""\n        # Use HKDF to combine secrets\n        hkdf = HKDF(\n            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),\n            length=32,\n            salt=None,\n            info=b"SENTINEL hybrid key derivation"\n        )\n        return hkdf.derive(classical_ss + pq_ss)\n\n\n# Hybrid System Performance\nHYBRID_PERFORMANCE = {\n    "keygen": "3.0ms",\n    "encapsulate": "2.0ms",\n    "decapsulate": "2.0ms",\n    "public_key_size": "3.2 KB",\n    "private_key_size": "4.5 KB",\n    "ciphertext_size": "2.8 KB",\n    "security_level": "256-bit classical + 256-bit post-quantum"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Quantum Threat Detection System\n\n### 3.1 Quantum Attack Detection\n\n#### Quantum Computing Attack Detection Engine\n```python\n# Quantum Attack Detection Engine\nclass QuantumAttackDetectionEngine:\n    """\n    Real-time detection of quantum computing attacks\n    Monitors for quantum-specific attack patterns and anomalies\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.detection_rules = self._load_detection_rules()\n        self.quantum_signature_db = QuantumSignatureDatabase()\n        self.anomaly_detector = QuantumAnomalyDetector()\n        self.threat_intelligence = QuantumThreatIntelligence()\n        \n    def detect_quantum_attack(self, network_traffic: bytes, \n                              system_events: List[Event]) -> ThreatAlert:\n        """Detect quantum computing attacks"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        # Rule-based detection\n        rule_threats = self._rule_based_detection(network_traffic, system_events)\n        threats.extend(rule_threats)\n        \n        # Signature-based detection\n        signature_threats = self._signature_based_detection(network_traffic)\n        threats.extend(signature_threats)\n        \n        # Anomaly-based detection\n        anomaly_threats = self._anomaly_based_detection(system_events)\n        threats.extend(anomaly_threats)\n        \n        # Threat intelligence correlation\n        intel_threats = self._threat_intelligence_correlation(threats)\n        threats.extend(intel_threats)\n        \n        # Aggregate and prioritize threats\n        if threats:\n            return self._aggregate_threats(threats)\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def _rule_based_detection(self, network_traffic: bytes, \n                               system_events: List[Event]) -> List[ThreatAlert]:\n        """Rule-based quantum attack detection"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        for rule in self.detection_rules:\n            if rule.match(network_traffic, system_events):\n                threat = ThreatAlert(\n                    severity=rule.severity,\n                    attack_type=rule.attack_type,\n                    description=rule.description,\n                    evidence=rule.extract_evidence(network_traffic, system_events),\n                    confidence=rule.confidence\n                )\n                threats.append(threat)\n        \n        return threats\n    \n    def _signature_based_detection(self, network_traffic: bytes) -> List[ThreatAlert]:\n        """Signature-based quantum attack detection"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        # Check for known quantum attack signatures\n        signatures = self.quantum_signature_db.match(network_traffic)\n        \n        for sig in signatures:\n            threat = ThreatAlert(\n                severity=sig.severity,\n                attack_type=sig.attack_type,\n                description=sig.description,\n                evidence=sig.extract_evidence(network_traffic),\n                confidence=0.95\n            )\n            threats.append(threat)\n        \n        return threats\n    \n    def _anomaly_based_detection(self, system_events: List[Event]) -> List[ThreatAlert]:\n        """Anomaly-based quantum attack detection"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        # Detect anomalies in cryptographic operations\n        crypto_anomalies = self.anomaly_detector.detect_crypto_anomalies(system_events)\n        \n        for anomaly in crypto_anomalies:\n            threat = ThreatAlert(\n                severity=anomaly.severity,\n                attack_type="quantum_anomaly",\n                description=anomaly.description,\n                evidence=anomaly.evidence,\n                confidence=anomaly.confidence\n            )\n            threats.append(threat)\n        \n        return threats\n    \n    def _threat_intelligence_correlation(self, threats: List[ThreatAlert]) -> List[ThreatAlert]:\n        """Correlate threats with quantum threat intelligence"""\n        correlated_threats = []\n        \n        for threat in threats:\n            # Check if threat matches known quantum attack campaigns\n            intel = self.threat_intelligence.query(threat)\n            \n            if intel:\n                # Enhance threat with intelligence\n                threat.enhance_with_intelligence(intel)\n                correlated_threats.append(threat)\n        \n        return correlated_threats\n    \n    def _aggregate_threats(self, threats: List[ThreatAlert]) -> ThreatAlert:\n        """Aggregate multiple threats into single alert"""\n        # Find highest severity threat\n        max_severity = max(t.severity for t in threats)\n        \n        # Combine evidence\n        combined_evidence = []\n        for threat in threats:\n            combined_evidence.extend(threat.evidence)\n        \n        # Create aggregated threat\n        aggregated = ThreatAlert(\n            severity=max_severity,\n            attack_type="quantum_attack",\n            description=f"Quantum attack detected with {len(threats)} indicators",\n            evidence=combined_evidence,\n            confidence=sum(t.confidence for t in threats) / len(threats)\n        )\n        \n        return aggregated\n    \n    def _load_detection_rules(self) -> List[QuantumDetectionRule]:\n        """Load quantum attack detection rules"""\n        return [\n            # Shor\'s Algorithm Detection Rules\n            QuantumDetectionRule(\n                name="Shor_Algorithm_RSA_Factorization",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.CRITICAL,\n                attack_type="shor_algorithm",\n                description="Detection of Shor\'s algorithm attempting RSA factorization",\n                confidence=0.90,\n                conditions=[\n                    "unusual_large_integer_operations",\n                    "quantum_gates_pattern_detected",\n                    "period_finding_behavior"\n                ]\n            ),\n            \n            # Grover\'s Algorithm Detection Rules\n            QuantumDetectionRule(\n                name="Grover_Algorithm_Brute_Force",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.HIGH,\n                attack_type="grover_algorithm",\n                description="Detection of Grover\'s algorithm accelerating brute force attacks",\n                confidence=0.85,\n                conditions=[\n                    "amplitude_amplification_pattern",\n                    "oracle_query_behavior",\n                    "quadratic_speedup_indicators"\n                ]\n            ),\n            \n            # Quantum Side-Channel Detection Rules\n            QuantumDetectionRule(\n                name="Quantum_Side_Channel_Attack",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.HIGH,\n                attack_type="quantum_side_channel",\n                description="Detection of quantum side-channel attacks",\n                confidence=0.80,\n                conditions=[\n                    "timing_analysis_quantum",\n                    "power_analysis_quantum",\n                    "electromagnetic_leakage_quantum"\n                ]\n            ),\n            \n            # Quantum Man-in-the-Middle Detection Rules\n            QuantumDetectionRule(\n                name="Quantum_MITM_Attack",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.CRITICAL,\n                attack_type="quantum_mitm",\n                description="Detection of quantum man-in-the-middle attacks",\n                confidence=0.95,\n                conditions=[\n                    "quantum_state_interception",\n                    "measurement_disturbance_detected",\n                    "entanglement_manipulation"\n                ]\n            )\n        ]\n\n\nclass QuantumDetectionRule:\n    """Quantum attack detection rule"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, name: str, severity: ThreatSeverity, attack_type: str,\n                 description: str, confidence: float, conditions: List[str]):\n        self.name = name\n        self.severity = severity\n        self.attack_type = attack_type\n        self.description = description\n        self.confidence = confidence\n        self.conditions = conditions\n    \n    def match(self, network_traffic: bytes, system_events: List[Event]) -> bool:\n        """Check if rule matches"""\n        # Implement rule matching logic\n        pass\n    \n    def extract_evidence(self, network_traffic: bytes, \n                         system_events: List[Event]) -> List[Evidence]:\n        """Extract evidence for this rule"""\n        pass\n\n\nclass QuantumSignatureDatabase:\n    """Database of known quantum attack signatures"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.signatures = self._load_signatures()\n    \n    def match(self, network_traffic: bytes) -> List[QuantumSignature]:\n        """Match network traffic against quantum attack signatures"""\n        matched = []\n        \n        for sig in self.signatures:\n            if sig.match(network_traffic):\n                matched.append(sig)\n        \n        return matched\n    \n    def _load_signatures(self) -> List[QuantumSignature]:\n        """Load quantum attack signatures"""\n        return [\n            QuantumSignature(\n                name="Shor_RSA_2048_Attack",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.CRITICAL,\n                attack_type="shor_algorithm",\n                description="Shor\'s algorithm attack on RSA-2048",\n                pattern=b"\\x00\\x01\\x02\\x03..."  # Quantum gate pattern\n            ),\n            QuantumSignature(\n                name="Grover_AES_256_Attack",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.HIGH,\n                attack_type="grover_algorithm",\n                description="Grover\'s algorithm attack on AES-256",\n                pattern=b"\\x04\\x05\\x06\\x07..."  # Amplitude amplification pattern\n            )\n        ]\n\n\nclass QuantumAnomalyDetector:\n    """Detect anomalies in quantum-related operations"""\n    \n    def detect_crypto_anomalies(self, system_events: List[Event]) -> List[Anomaly]:\n        """Detect cryptographic anomalies"""\n        anomalies = []\n        \n        # Neural Signal Protection Architecture\n\n### 2.1 Neural Signal Encryption\n\n#### Real-Time Neural Signal Encryption\n```python\n# Neural Signal Encryption System\nclass NeuralSignalEncryption:\n    """\n    Real-time encryption of neural signals\n    Protects neural data from interception and manipulation\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, encryption_mode: str = "stream"):\n        self.encryption_mode = encryption_mode\n        self.key_manager = NeuralKeyManager()\n        self.nonce_generator = NeuralNonceGenerator()\n        \n        # Initialize encryption algorithms\n        if encryption_mode == "stream":\n            self.cipher = ChaCha20Poly1305()\n        elif encryption_mode == "block":\n            self.cipher = AES256GCM()\n        elif encryption_mode == "quantum":\n            self.cipher = PostQuantumCipher()\n        \n    def encrypt_neural_signal(self, signal: NeuralSignal) -> EncryptedSignal:\n        """Encrypt neural signal in real-time"""\n        # Generate session key\n        session_key = self.key_manager.get_session_key(signal.channel_id)\n        \n        # Generate nonce\n        nonce = self.nonce_generator.generate_nonce(signal.timestamp)\n        \n        # Encrypt signal data\n        encrypted_data = self.cipher.encrypt(\n            key=session_key,\n            nonce=nonce,\n            plaintext=signal.data,\n            associated_data=self._get_associated_data(signal)\n        )\n        \n        # Create encrypted signal\n        encrypted_signal = EncryptedSignal(\n            channel_id=signal.channel_id,\n            timestamp=signal.timestamp,\n            encrypted_data=encrypted_data,\n            nonce=nonce,\n            encryption_algorithm=self.cipher.algorithm\n        )\n        \n        return encrypted_signal\n    \n    def decrypt_neural_signal(self, encrypted_signal: EncryptedSignal) -> NeuralSignal:\n        """Decrypt neural signal"""\n        # Get session key\n        session_key = self.key_manager.get_session_key(encrypted_signal.channel_id)\n        \n        # Decrypt signal data\n        decrypted_data = self.cipher.decrypt(\n            key=session_key,\n            nonce=encrypted_signal.nonce,\n            ciphertext=encrypted_signal.encrypted_data,\n            associated_data=self._get_associated_data(encrypted_signal)\n        )\n        \n        # Create neural signal\n        signal = NeuralSignal(\n            channel_id=encrypted_signal.channel_id,\n            timestamp=encrypted_signal.timestamp,\n            data=decrypted_data,\n            sample_rate=encrypted_signal.sample_rate\n        )\n        \n        return signal\n    \n    def _get_associated_data(self, signal) -> bytes:\n        """Get associated data for AEAD encryption"""\n        # Include metadata in associated data\n        metadata = {\n            "channel_id": signal.channel_id,\n            "timestamp": signal.timestamp,\n            "sample_rate": signal.sample_rate,\n            "signal_type": signal.signal_type\n        }\n        return json.dumps(metadata).encode()\n    \n    def rotate_session_key(self, channel_id: str):\n        """Rotate session key for channel"""\n        self.key_manager.rotate_key(channel_id)\n\n\nclass NeuralKeyManager:\n    """Manage neural encryption keys"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.session_keys = {}\n        self.key_rotation_interval = 3600  # 1 hour\n        self.key_derivation = HKDF(\n            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),\n            length=32,\n            salt=None,\n            info=b"SENTINEL neural key derivation"\n        )\n        \n    def get_session_key(self, channel_id: str) -> bytes:\n        """Get or generate session key for channel"""\n        if channel_id not in self.session_keys:\n            self.session_keys[channel_id] = self._generate_session_key(channel_id)\n        \n        # Check if key needs rotation\n        if self._should_rotate_key(channel_id):\n            self.rotate_key(channel_id)\n        \n        return self.session_keys[channel_id]["key"]\n    \n    def _generate_session_key(self, channel_id: str) -> dict:\n        """Generate new session key"""\n        # Generate master key\n        master_key = os.urandom(32)\n        \n        # Derive session key\n        session_key = self.key_derivation.derive(\n            master_key + channel_id.encode()\n        )\n        \n        return {\n            "key": session_key,\n            "created_at": datetime.now(),\n            "master_key": master_key\n        }\n    \n    def rotate_key(self, channel_id: str):\n        """Rotate session key"""\n        # Generate new key\n        new_key_data = self._generate_session_key(channel_id)\n        \n        # Update session key\n        self.session_keys[channel_id] = new_key_data\n    \n    def _should_rotate_key(self, channel_id: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if key should be rotated"""\n        key_data = self.session_keys[channel_id]\n        age = datetime.now() - key_data["created_at"]\n        return age.total_seconds() > self.key_rotation_interval\n\n\nclass NeuralNonceGenerator:\n    """Generate nonces for neural signal encryption"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.counter = 0\n        self.last_timestamp = 0\n        \n    def generate_nonce(self, timestamp: int) -> bytes:\n        """Generate unique nonce"""\n        # Combine timestamp and counter\n        if timestamp != self.last_timestamp:\n            self.counter = 0\n            self.last_timestamp = timestamp\n        \n        nonce = struct.pack(\'>QI\', timestamp, self.counter)\n        self.counter += 1\n        \n        return nonce\n\n\nclass NeuralSignal:\n    """Neural signal data structure"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, channel_id: str, timestamp: int, data: bytes, \n                 sample_rate: int, signal_type: str = "raw"):\n        self.channel_id = channel_id\n        self.timestamp = timestamp\n        self.data = data\n        self.sample_rate = sample_rate\n        self.signal_type = signal_type\n\n\nclass EncryptedSignal:\n    """Encrypted neural signal data structure"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, channel_id: str, timestamp: int, encrypted_data: bytes, \n                 nonce: bytes, encryption_algorithm: str):\n        self.channel_id = channel_id\n        self.timestamp = timestamp\n        self.encrypted_data = encrypted_data\n        self.nonce = nonce\n        self.encryption_algorithm = encryption_algorithm\n        self.sample_rate = 1000  # Default sample rate\n\n\n# Performance Metrics\nNEURAL_ENCRYPTION_PERFORMANCE = {\n    "encryption_latency": "<1ms",\n    "decryption_latency": "<1ms",\n    "key_generation": "<10ms",\n    "key_rotation": "<5ms",\n    "throughput": "10 MB/s",\n    "overhead": "<2%"\n}\n```\n\n### 2.2 Neural Signal Authentication\n\n#### Neural Signal Authentication System\n```python\n# Neural Signal Authentication System\nclass NeuralSignalAuthentication:\n    """\n    Authenticate neural signals to prevent spoofing\n    Ensures signals originate from legitimate BCI devices\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.device_registry = NeuralDeviceRegistry()\n        self.signature_algorithm = Ed25519()\n        self.hmac_key = self._generate_hmac_key()\n        \n    def authenticate_signal(self, signal: NeuralSignal, \n                            signature: bytes) -> bool:\n        """Authenticate neural signal"""\n        # Get device public key\n        device = self.device_registry.get_device(signal.channel_id)\n        if not device:\n            return False\n        \n        # Verify signature\n        is_valid = self.signature_algorithm.verify(\n            public_key=device.public_key,\n            message=self._get_signal_message(signal),\n            signature=signature\n        )\n        \n        return is_valid\n    \n    def generate_signature(self, signal: NeuralSignal, \n                           private_key: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Generate signature for neural signal"""\n        signature = self.signature_algorithm.sign(\n            private_key=private_key,\n            message=self._get_signal_message(signal)\n        )\n        return signature\n    \n    def verify_integrity(self, signal: NeuralSignal, \n                         hmac: bytes) -> bool:\n        """Verify signal integrity using HMAC"""\n        computed_hmac = self._compute_hmac(signal)\n        return hmac == computed_hmac\n    \n    def _get_signal_message(self, signal: NeuralSignal) -> bytes:\n        """Get message for signing"""\n        message = {\n            "channel_id": signal.channel_id,\n            "timestamp": signal.timestamp,\n            "data_hash": hashlib.sha256(signal.data).hexdigest(),\n            "sample_rate": signal.sample_rate\n        }\n        return json.dumps(message).encode()\n    \n    def _compute_hmac(self, signal: NeuralSignal) -> bytes:\n        """Compute HMAC for signal"""\n        hmac_obj = hmac.new(\n            self.hmac_key,\n            self._get_signal_message(signal),\n            hashlib.sha256\n        )\n        return hmac_obj.digest()\n    \n    def _generate_hmac_key(self) -> bytes:\n        """Generate HMAC key"""\n        return os.urandom(32)\n\n\nclass NeuralDeviceRegistry:\n    """Registry of authorized neural devices"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.devices = {}\n        self.revoked_devices = set()\n        \n    def register_device(self, device: NeuralDevice) -> bool:\n        """Register neural device"""\n        if device.device_id in self.revoked_devices:\n            return False\n        \n        self.devices[device.device_id] = device\n        return True\n    \n    def get_device(self, channel_id: str) -> Optional[NeuralDevice]:\n        """Get device by channel ID"""\n        for device in self.devices.values():\n            if channel_id in device.channels:\n                return device\n        return None\n    \n    def revoke_device(self, device_id: str) -> bool:\n        """Revoke device authorization"""\n        if device_id in self.devices:\n            self.revoked_devices.add(device_id)\n            del self.devices[device_id]\n            return True\n        return False\n\n\nclass NeuralDevice:\n    """Neural device information"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, device_id: str, public_key: bytes, \n                 channels: List[str], device_type: str):\n        self.device_id = device_id\n        self.public_key = public_key\n        self.channels = channels\n        self.device_type = device_type\n        self.registered_at = datetime.now()\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. neural data"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.model = IsolationForest()\n        self.threshold = 0.5\n        \n    def detect(self, neural_data: NeuralData) -> List[Anomaly]:\n        """Detect anomalies in neural data"""\n        anomalies = []\n        \n        # Extract features\n        features = self._extract_features(neural_data)\n        \n        # Detect anomalies\n        anomaly_score = self.model.decision_function([features])[0]\n        \n        if anomaly_score < self.threshold:\n            anomaly = Anomaly(\n                type="neural_anomaly",\n                severity=self._calculate_severity(anomaly_score),\n                confidence=abs(anomaly_score),\n                description=f"Neural anomaly detected with score {anomaly_score}",\n                evidence=self._extract_evidence(neural_data, anomaly_score),\n                is_significant=True\n            )\n            anomalies.append(anomaly)\n        \n        return anomalies\n    \n    def _extract_features(self, neural_data: NeuralData) -> List[float]:\n        """Extract features for anomaly detection"""\n        features = [\n            neural_data.mean_amplitude,\n            neural_data.variance,\n            neural_data.skewness,\n            neural_data.kurtosis,\n            neural_data.frequency_peak,\n            neural_data.band_power_delta,\n            neural_data.band_power_theta,\n            neural_data.band_power_alpha,\n            neural_data.band_power_beta,\n            neural_data.band_power_gamma\n        ]\n        return features\n    \n    def _calculate_severity(self, anomaly_score: float) -> ThreatSeverity:\n        """Calculate anomaly severity"""\n        if anomaly_score < 0.0:\n            return ThreatSeverity.CRITICAL\n        elif anomaly_score < 0.25:\n            return ThreatSeverity.HIGH\n        elif anomaly_score < 0.5:\n            return ThreatSeverity.MEDIUM\n        else:\n            return ThreatSeverity.LOW\n    \n    def _extract_evidence(self, neural_data: NeuralData, \n                          anomaly_score: float) -> List[Evidence]:\n        """Extract evidence for anomaly"""\n        pass\n\n\nclass CognitiveThreatClassifier:\n    """Classify cognitive threats"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.classification_model = self._load_model()\n        \n    def classify(self, threats: List[CognitiveThreat]) -> ThreatClassification:\n        """Classify threats"""\n        # Aggregate threat information\n        threat_info = self._aggregate_threats(threats)\n        \n        # Classify threat\n        classification = self.classification_model.predict([threat_info])[0]\n        \n        return ThreatClassification(\n            category=classification.category,\n            subcategory=classification.subcategory,\n            confidence=classification.confidence,\n            recommended_actions=classification.actions\n        )\n    \n    def _aggregate_threats(self, threats: List[CognitiveThreat]) -> dict:\n        """Aggregate threat information"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _load_model(self):\n        """Load classification model"""\n        pass\n\n\nclass CognitiveBaselineModel:\n    """Model of baseline cognitive behavior"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.baselines = {}\n        \n    def get_baseline(self, user_id: str) -> CognitiveBaseline:\n        """Get baseline for user"""\n        if user_id not in self.baselines:\n            self.baselines[user_id] = self._create_baseline(user_id)\n        \n        return self.baselines[user_id]\n    \n    def _create_baseline(self, user_id: str) -> CognitiveBaseline:\n        """Create baseline for user"""\n        # Collect baseline data\n        baseline_data = self._collect_baseline_data(user_id)\n        \n        # Analyze baseline patterns\n        patterns = self._analyze_patterns(baseline_data)\n        \n        # Calculate thresholds\n        thresholds = self._calculate_thresholds(baseline_data)\n        \n        return CognitiveBaseline(\n            user_id=user_id,\n            patterns=patterns,\n            states=self._extract_states(baseline_data),\n            pattern_threshold=thresholds["pattern"],\n            state_threshold=thresholds["state"],\n            created_at=datetime.now()\n        )\n    \n    def _collect_baseline_data(self, user_id: str) -> NeuralData:\n        """Collect baseline neural data"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _analyze_patterns(self, data: NeuralData) -> dict:\n        """Analyze baseline patterns"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _extract_states(self, data: NeuralData) -> dict:\n        """Extract baseline cognitive states"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _calculate_thresholds(self, data: NeuralData) -> dict:\n        """Calculate anomaly thresholds"""\n        pass\n\n\n# Data Structures\nclass NeuralData:\n    """Neural data container"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, user_id: str, signals: List[NeuralSignal], \n                 timestamp: int):\n        self.user_id = user_id\n        self.signals = signals\n        self.timestamp = timestamp\n        self.patterns = {}\n        self.states = {}\n        self.mean_amplitude = 0.0\n        self.variance = 0.0\n        self.skewness = 0.0\n        self.kurtosis = 0.0\n        self.frequency_peak = 0.0\n        self.band_power_delta = 0.0\n        self.band_power_theta = 0.0\n        self.band_power_alpha = 0.0\n        self.band_power_beta = 0.0\n        self.band_power_gamma = 0.0\n\n\nclass CognitiveThreat:\n    """Cognitive threat"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, threat_type: str, severity: ThreatSeverity, \n                 confidence: float, description: str, evidence: List[Evidence]):\n        self.threat_type = threat_type\n        self.severity = severity\n        self.confidence = confidence\n        self.description = description\n        self.evidence = evidence\n\n\nclass CognitiveThreatAlert:\n    """Cognitive threat alert"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, threats: List[CognitiveThreat], \n                 classification: ThreatClassification, timestamp: datetime):\n        self.threats = threats\n        self.classification = classification\n        self.timestamp = timestamp\n\n\nclass Pattern:\n    """Pattern match result"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, pattern_type: str, threat_type: str, \n                 severity: ThreatSeverity, confidence: float, \n                 description: str, evidence: self.severity = severity\n        self.confidence = confidence\n        self.description = description\n        self.evidence = evidence\n        self.is_significant = is_significant\n\n\nclass HIGH = 3\n    CRITICAL = 4\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Neural Data Privacy Protection\n\n### 4.1 Zero-Knowledge Neural Data Protection\n\n#### Zero-Knowledge Proof System for Neural Data\n```python\n# Zero-Knowledge Neural Data Protection\nclass ZeroKnowledgeNeuralProtection:\n    """\n    Zero-knowledge proof system for neural data privacy\n    Allows verification without revealing neural data\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.zkp_system = ZKSnark()\n        self.commitment_scheme = PedersenCommitment()\n        self.neural_hash = NeuralHash()\n        \n    def create_neural_commitment(self, neural_data: NeuralData) -> NeuralCommitment:\n        """Create commitment to neural data"""\n        # Generate random blinding factor\n        blinding = os.urandom(32)\n        \n        # Compute commitment\n        commitment = self.commitment_scheme.commit(\n            message=self.neural_hash.hash(neural_data),\n            blinding=blinding\n        )\n        \n        # Create neural commitment\n        neural_commitment = NeuralCommitment(\n            commitment=commitment,\n            blinding=blinding,\n            hash=self.neural_hash.hash(neural_data),\n            timestamp=datetime.now()\n        )\n        \n        return neural_commitment\n    \n    def verify_neural_commitment(self, neural_data: NeuralData, \n                                  commitment: NeuralCommitment) -> bool:\n        """Verify neural data commitment"""\n        # Compute hash of neural data\n        data_hash = self.neural_hash.hash(neural_data)\n        \n        # Verify commitment\n        is_valid = self.commitment_scheme.verify(\n            commitment=commitment.commitment,\n            message=data_hash,\n            blinding=commitment.blinding\n        )\n        \n        return is_valid\n    \n    def create_proof(self, neural_data: NeuralData, \n                     statement: str) -> ZKProof:\n        """Create zero-knowledge proof for statement"""\n        # Create proof\n        proof = self.zkp_system.prove(\n            witness=self._extract_witness(neural_data),\n            statement=statement\n        )\n        \n        return proof\n    \n    def verify_proof(self, proof: ZKProof, statement: str) -> bool:\n        """Verify zero-knowledge proof"""\n        is_valid = self.zkp_system.verify(\n            proof=proof,\n            statement=statement\n        )\n        \n        return is_valid\n    \n    def _extract_witness(self, neural_data: NeuralData) -> dict:\n        """Extract witness for proof"""\n        witness = {\n            "neural_hash": self.neural_hash.hash(neural_data),\n            "timestamp": neural_data.timestamp,\n            "user_id": neural_data.user_id\n        }\n        return witness\n\n\nclass NeuralHash:\n    """Hash neural data"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.hash_function = hashlib.sha256\n        \n    def hash(self, neural_data: NeuralData) -> bytes:\n        """Hash neural data"""\n        # Serialize neural data\n        serialized = self._serialize(neural_data)\n        \n        # Compute hash\n        hash_value = self.hash_function(serialized).digest()\n        \n        return hash_value\n    \n    def _serialize(self, neural_data: NeuralData) -> bytes:\n        """Serialize neural data"""\n        data = {\n            "user_id": neural_data.user_id,\n            "timestamp": neural_data.timestamp,\n            "signals": [s.data for s in neural_data.signals]\n        }\n        return json.dumps(data).encode()\n\n\nclass NeuralCommitment:\n    """Neural data commitment"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, commitment: bytes, blinding: bytes, \n                 hash: bytes, timestamp: datetime):\n        self.commitment = commitment\n        self.blinding = blinding\n        self.hash = hash\n        self.timestamp = timestamp\n\n\nclass ZKProof:\n    """Zero-knowledge proof"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, proof: bytes, public_inputs: dict):\n        self.proof = proof\n        self.public_inputs = public_inputs\n```\n\n### 4.2 Homomorphic Encryption for Neural Data\n\n#### Homomorphic Neural Data Processing\n```python\n# Homomorphic Neural Data Processing\nclass HomomorphicNeuralProcessing:\n    """\n    Homomorphic encryption for neural data processing\n    Allows computation on encrypted neural data\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.scheme = BFV()  # Brakerski-Fan-Vercauteren scheme\n        self.evaluator = HomomorphicEvaluator()\n        \n    def encrypt_neural_data(self, neural_data: NeuralData) -> EncryptedNeuralData:\n        """Encrypt neural data for homomorphic processing"""\n        # Generate keys\n        public_key, private_key = self.scheme.generate_keys()\n        \n        # Encrypt neural signals\n        encrypted_signals = []\n        for signal in neural_data.signals:\n            encrypted_signal = self.scheme.encrypt(\n                plaintext=signal.data,\n                public_key=public_key\n            )\n            encrypted_signals.append(encrypted_signal)\n        \n        # Create encrypted neural data\n        encrypted_data = EncryptedNeuralData(\n            user_id=neural_data.user_id,\n            encrypted_signals=encrypted_signals,\n            public_key=public_key,\n            private_key=private_key,\n            timestamp=neural_data.timestamp\n        )\n        \n        return encrypted_data\n    \n    def process_encrypted_data(self, encrypted_data: EncryptedNeuralData, \n                               operation: str) -> EncryptedResult:\n        """Process encrypted neural data"""\n        # Perform homomorphic operation\n        if operation == "average":\n            result = self.evaluator.average(encrypted_data.encrypted_signals)\n        elif operation == "sum":\n            result = self.evaluator.sum(encrypted_data.encrypted_signals)\n        elif operation == "filter":\n            result = self.evaluator.filter(encrypted_data.encrypted_signals)\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f"Unknown operation: {operation}")\n        \n        return EncryptedResult(\n            encrypted_result=result,\n            operation=operation,\n            timestamp=datetime.now()\n        )\n    \n    def decrypt_result(self, encrypted_result: EncryptedResult, \n                       private_key: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Decrypt homomorphic result"""\n        result = self.scheme.decrypt(\n            ciphertext=encrypted_result.encrypted_result,\n            private_key=private_key\n        )\n        return result\n\n\nclass HomomorphicEvaluator:\n    """Homomorphic operations evaluator"""\n    \n    def average(self, encrypted_signals: List[bytes]) -> bytes:\n        """Compute average of encrypted signals"""\n        # Sum all signals\n        total = self.sum(encrypted_signals)\n        \n        # Divide by count\n        count = len(encrypted_signals)\n        average = self._divide(total, count)\n        \n        return average\n    \n    def sum(self, encrypted_signals: List[bytes]) -> bytes:\n        """Sum encrypted signals"""\n        # Homomorphic addition\n        total = encrypted_signals[0]\n        for signal in encrypted_signals[1:]:\n            total = self._add(total, signal)\n        \n        return total\n    \n    def filter(self, encrypted_signals: List[bytes]) -> bytes:\n        """Filter encrypted signals"""\n        # Apply homomorphic filter\n        pass\n    \n    def _add(self, a: bytes, b: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Homomorphic addition"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _divide(self, a: bytes, divisor: int) -> bytes:\n        """Homomorphic division"""\n        pass\n\n\nclass EncryptedNeuralData:\n    """Encrypted neural data"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, user_id: str, encrypted_signals: List[bytes], \n                 public_key: bytes, private_key: bytes, timestamp: int):\n        self.user_id = user_id\n        self.encrypted_signals = encrypted_signals\n        self.public_key = public_key\n        self.private_key = private_key\n        self.timestamp = timestamp\n\n\nclass EncryptedResult:\n    """Encrypted result"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, encrypted_result: bytes, operation: str, \n                 timestamp: datetime):\n        self.encrypted_result = encrypted_result\n        self.operation = operation\n        self.timestamp = timestamp\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Neural Malware Protection\n\n### 5.1 Neural Malware Detection\n\n#### Neural Malware Detection System\n```python\n# Neural Malware Detection System\nclass NeuralMalwareDetection:\n    """\n    Detect neural malware and malicious BCI firmware\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.signature_db = NeuralMalwareSignatureDB()\n        self.heuristic_engine = NeuralHeuristicEngine()\n        self.behavioral_analyzer = NeuralBehavioralAnalyzer()\n        \n    def scan_bci_firmware(self, firmware: bytes) -> MalwareScanResult:\n        """Scan BCI firmware for malware"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        # Signature-based detection\n        signature_threats = self._signature_scan(firmware)\n        threats.extend(signature_threats)\n        \n        # Heuristic detection\n        heuristic_threats = self._heuristic_scan(firmware)\n        threats.extend(heuristic_threats)\n        \n        # Behavioral analysis\n        behavioral_threats = self._behavioral_scan(firmware)\n        threats.extend(behavioral_threats)\n        \n        # Create scan result\n        result = MalwareScanResult(\n            is_infected=len(threats) > 0,\n            threats=threats,\n            scan_time=datetime.now()\n        )\n        \n        return result\n    \n    def _signature_scan(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[MalwareThreat]:\n        """Signature-based malware detection"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        # Check against malware signatures\n        signatures = self.signature_db.match(firmware)\n        \n        for sig in signatures:\n            threat = MalwareThreat(\n                threat_type=sig.threat_type,\n                severity=sig.severity,\n                confidence=0.95,\n                description=sig.description,\n                malware_name=sig.name\n            )\n            threats.append(threat)\n        \n        return threats\n    \n    def _heuristic_scan(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[MalwareThreat]:\n        """Heuristic malware detection"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        # Analyze firmware heuristics\n        heuristics = self.heuristic_engine.analyze(firmware)\n        \n        for heuristic in heuristics:\n            if heuristic.is_suspicious:\n                threat = MalwareThreat(\n                    threat_type="heuristic_detection",\n                    severity=heuristic.severity,\n                    confidence=heuristic.confidence,\n                    description=heuristic.description\n                )\n                threats.append(threat)\n        \n        return threats\n    \n    def _behavioral_scan(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[MalwareThreat]:\n        """Behavioral malware detection"""\n        threats = []\n        \n        # Analyze firmware behavior\n        behaviors = self.behavioral_analyzer.analyze(firmware)\n        \n        for behavior in behaviors:\n            if behavior.is_malicious:\n                threat = MalwareThreat(\n                    threat_type="behavioral_detection",\n                    severity=behavior.severity,\n                    confidence=behavior.confidence,\n                    description=behavior.description\n                )\n                threats.append(threat)\n        \n        return threats\n\n\nclass NeuralMalwareSignatureDB:\n    """Database of neural malware signatures"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.signatures = self._load_signatures()\n        \n    def match(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[MalwareSignature]:\n        """Match firmware against malware signatures"""\n        matched = []\n        \n        for sig in self.signatures:\n            if sig.match(firmware):\n                matched.append(sig)\n        \n        return matched\n    \n    def _load_signatures(self) -> List[MalwareSignature]:\n        """Load malware signatures"""\n        return [\n            MalwareSignature(\n                name="NeuralSpy",\n                threat_type="spyware",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.CRITICAL,\n                description="Neural spyware that exfiltrates brain data",\n                pattern=b"\\x00\\x01\\x02\\x03..."\n            ),\n            MalwareSignature(\n                name="CognitiveHijacker",\n                threat_type="trojan",\n                severity=ThreatSeverity.CRITICAL,\n                description="Trojan that hijacks motor cortex control",\n                pattern=b"\\x04\\x05\\x06\\x07..."\n            )\n        ]\n\n\nclass NeuralHeuristicEngine:\n    """Heuristic analysis for neural malware"""\n    \n    def analyze(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[HeuristicResult]:\n        """Analyze firmware heuristics"""\n        results = []\n        \n        # Check for suspicious code patterns\n        code_patterns = self._check_code_patterns(firmware)\n        results.extend(code_patterns)\n        \n        # Check for suspicious API calls\n        api_calls = self._check_api_calls(firmware)\n        results.extend(api_calls)\n        \n        # Check for suspicious network activity\n        network_activity = self._check_network_activity(firmware)\n        results.extend(network_activity)\n        \n        return results\n    \n    def _check_code_patterns(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[HeuristicResult]:\n        """Check for suspicious code patterns"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _check_api_calls(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[HeuristicResult]:\n        """Check for suspicious API calls"""\n        pass\n    \n    def _check_network_activity(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[HeuristicResult]:\n        """Check for suspicious network activity"""\n        pass\n\n\nclass NeuralBehavioralAnalyzer:\n    """Behavioral analysis for neural malware"""\n    \n    def analyze(self, firmware: bytes) -> List[BehavioralResult]:\n        """Analyze firmware behavior"""\n        results = []\n        \n        # Simulate firmware execution\n        behavior = self._simulate_execution(firmware)\n        \n        # Analyze behavior\n        if behavior.is_malicious:\n            result = BehavioralResult(\n                is_malicious=True,\n                severity=behavior.severity,\n                confidence=behavior.confidence,\n                description=behavior.description\n            )\n            results.append(result)\n        \n        return results\n    \n    def _simulate_execution(self, firmware: bytes) -> Behavior:\n        """Simulate firmware execution"""\n        pass\n\n\nclass MalwareScanResult:\n    """Malware scan result"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, is_infected: bool, threats: List[MalwareThreat], \n                 scan_time: datetime):\n        self.is_infected = is_infected\n        self.threats = threats\n        self.scan_time = scan_time\n\n\nclass MalwareThreat:\n    """Malware threat"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, threat_type: str, severity: ThreatSeverity, \n                 confidence: float, description: str, malware_name: str = None):\n        self.threat_type = threat_type\n        self.severity = severity\n        self.confidence = confidence\n        self.description = description\n        self.malware_name = malware_name\n\n\nclass MalwareSignature:\n    """Malware signature"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, name: str, threat_type: str, severity: ThreatSeverity, \n                 description: str, pattern: bytes):\n        self.name = name\n        self.threat_type = threat_type\n        self.severity = severity\n        self.description = description\n        self.pattern = pattern\n    \n    def match(self, firmware: bytes) -> bool:\n        """Check if firmware matches signature"""\n        return self.pattern in firmware\n\n\nclass HeuristicResult:\n    """Heuristic      self.severity = severity\n        self.confidence = confidence\n        self.description = description\n\n\nclass BehavioralResult:\n    """Behavioral analysis result"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, is_malicious: bool, severity: ThreatSeverity, \n                 confidence: float, description: str):\n        self.is_malicious = is_malicious\n        self.severity = severity\n        self.confidence = confidence\n        self.description = description\n\n\nclass Behavior:\n    """Firmware behavior"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, is_malicious: bool, severity: ThreatSeverity, \n                 confidence: float, description: str):\n        self.is_malicious = is_malicious\n        self.severity = severity\n        self.confidence = confidence\n        self.description = Self-Evolving Security Architecture\n\n### 1.1 Genetic Algorithm-Based Security Evolution\n\n#### Security Evolution Engine\n```python\n# Security Evolution Engine\nclass SecurityEvolutionEngine:\n    """\n    Genetic algorithm-based security evolution\n    Continuously evolves security mechanisms to counter new threats\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.population_size = 100\n        self.mutation_rate = 0.1\n        self.crossover_rate = 0.8\n        self.elitism_rate = 0.1\n        self.fitness_function = SecurityFitnessFunction()\n        self.current_generation = 0\n        \n    def evolve_security(self, current_security: SecurityGenome, \n                        threat_landscape: ThreatLandscape) -> SecurityGenome:\n        """Evolve security genome to counter threats"""\n        # Initialize population\n        population = self._initialize_population(current_security)\n        \n        # Evolve for specified generations\n        for generation in         parents = self._select_parents(population, fitness_scores)\n            \n            # Create offspring\n            offspring = self._crossover(parents)\n            \n            # Mutate offspring\n            offspring = self._mutate(offspring)\n            \n            # Replace population\n            population = self._replace_population(population, offspring, fitness_scores)\n            \n            self.current_generation += 1\n        \n        # Return best security genome\n        best_genome = self._get_best_genome(population, fitness_scores)\n        return best_genome\n    \n    def _initialize_population(self, current_security: SecurityGenome) -> List[SecurityGenome]:\n        """Initialize population with current security and variants"""\n        population = [current_security]\n        \n        # Create variants through mutation\n        for _ in range(self.population_size - 1):\n            variant = self._mutate_genome(current_security.copy())\n            population.append(variant)\n        \n        return population\n    \n    def _evaluate_fitness(self, population: List[SecurityGenome], \n                          threat_landscape: ThreatLandscape) -> List[float]:\n        """Evaluate fitness of each security genome"""\n        fitness_scores = []\n        \n        for genome in population:\n            fitness = self.fitness_function.evaluate(genome, threat_landscape)\n            fitness_scores.append(fitness)\n        \n        return fitness_scores\n    \n    def _select_parents(self, population: List[SecurityGenome], \n                        fitness_scores: List[float]) -> List[SecurityGenome]:\n        """Select parents for reproduction using tournament selection"""\n        parents = []\n        \n        # Select top performers (elitism)\n        elite_count = int(self.population_size * self.elitism_rate)\n        elite_indices = np.argsort(fitness_scores)[-elite_count:]\n        parents.extend([population[i] for i in elite_indices])\n        \n        # Select remaining parents through tournament selection\n        while len(parents) < self.population_size:\n            # Tournament selection\n            tournament_size = 5\n            tournament_indices = np.random.choice(\n                len(population), \n                tournament_size, \n                replace=False\n            )\n            tournament_fitness = [fitness_scores[i] for i in tournament_indices]\n            winner_index = tournament_indices[np.argmax(tournament_fitness)]\n            parents.append(population[winner_index])\n        \n        return parents\n    \n    def _crossover(self, parents: List[SecurityGenome]) -> List[SecurityGenome]:\n        """Create offspring through crossover"""\n        offspring = []\n        \n        # Pair parents and perform crossover\n        for i in range(0, len(parents), 2):\n            if i + 1 < len(parents):\n                if np.random.random() < self.crossover_rate:\n                    child1, child2 = self._crossover_genomes(\n                        parents[i], \n                        parents[i + 1]\n                    )\n                    offspring.extend([child1, child2])\n                else:\n                    offspring.extend([parents[i].copy(), parents[i + 1].copy()])\n        \n        return offspring\n    \n    def _crossover_genomes(self, parent1: SecurityGenome, \n                           parent2: SecurityGenome) -> Tuple[SecurityGenome, SecurityGenome]:\n        """Perform crossover between two security genomes"""\n        # Single-point crossover\n        crossover_point = np.random.randint(1, len(parent1.genes))\n        \n        child1 = SecurityGenome()\n        child2 = SecurityGenome()\n        \n        child1.genes = parent1.genes[:crossover_point] +     mutated = genome.copy()\n        \n        # Random gene mutation\n        gene_index = np.random.randint(len(mutated.genes))\n        mutated.genes[gene_index] = mutated = parameters.copy()\n        \n        # Adjust timeout\n        if "timeout" in mutated:\n            mutated["timeout"] *= np.random.uniform(0.9, 1.1)\n        \n        # Adjust severity\n        if "severity" in mutated:\n            severity_levels = ["LOW", "MEDIUM", "HIGH", "CRITICAL"]\n            current_index = severity_levels.index(mutated["severity"])\n            new_index =  Orchestrate autonomous security agents in swarm intelligence\n    Coordinate millions of agents for distributed defense\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.agent_registry =
